padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2254013">hunybunbun</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-04"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730753942" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Imagination very much reminds me of Bvlgari Pour Homme, especially the tea note and dry down.  NOT surprised the nose is the same behind the two.   Imagination was created in 2021 and Bvlgari Pour Homme 1998.   All of Jacques Cavallier Belletrud's perfume experience and talent shows itself in Imagination.  It's like the flamboyant more traveled and much hipper younger brother to the Bvlgari.  People say it's "generic" but, to me, what they may be experiencing is the artists work from all the years before.  There is nothing generic about that luxurious tea note in the dry down.  <br />
<br />
The price is outrageous or it's a 10/10 for clean and freshies.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2337963"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2337963#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2337629" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Very citrusy and soapy and clean but nothing special. Now the drydown is something serious, I believe the tea note must have something to do with it. Such an interesting drydown, one of the best I’ve ever smelled. It’s a shame summer is over and it’s practically unwearable until mid-March/April, I’ll see you in a few months love</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2337629"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2337629#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2337459" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2204376">xth3hoff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-04"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730718935" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>LV imagination<br />
SCENT: ✨🫧☀️⚡️bright bubbly lemon and orange and sort of mandarin🍋🍊🍋🟩 combo of citrus, i believe what gives this fragrance a bubbly sprite feel is the 💦✨Citron note ,very unique to other generic citrus fragrances on the market which also makes this very addictive and stays throughout the duration of the wearing. Very good touch. What elevates this fragrance more is the electric⚡️🫚 vibe the ginger gives which is well complemented by the cinnamon which is well perfectly toned to which the neroli thats sits in the back which brings this together well. what does it for me that makes this fragrance so classy beautiful and sophisticated is the Chinese black tea and ambroxan which is also complemented well by slightly herbal frankincense and guaiac 🪵wood -(the woody elements are brilliant , its slight but there and plays very well) -which makes it a rlly nice fresh slightly herbal dry down by all means addicting and well done, this is a new level of fresh summer fragrance that can be worn on warmer seasons days, night even on dates its overall very bubbly lively and bright with a lovely fresh tea vibe on the dry down to some the opening might not make them see this as too special ,but as this fragrances settles more its a whole new field. A masterpiece.10/10 scent<br />
<br />
performance<br />
 For a more fresh and citrus fragrance this performs pretty well, the projection and silage was much more decent that i thought in the 4-6 hours range and dies down slightly slowly closer to your skin after to the 6hr but the first 4 are pretty well about more than an arms length ,which comes to the longevity 10+ hrs ,by now a skin scent but definitely still there , pretty impressive for this class of fragrance , the performance is definitely boosted due to the base of imagination. overall decent performance but impressive for the class its in. 8.5/10 - 9/10 (for a freshie citrus)<br />
<br />
in summary best fragrance of the summer freshie type of all time but it is abit pricey but is perfect for all occasions year round worth it in my opinion due to refills being available at Luis Vuitton boutique for about north of half price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It last long while not changing the smell too much.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2334094"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2334094#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2333728" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2333728" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Schoeibksr"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2283278"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2283278.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Schoeibksr" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2333728ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2333728" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2283278">Schoeibksr</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-31">10/31/24 12:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My perfect all season, all occasion fragrance. Meets every citrusy nerve in me. Jacques Cavallier-Belletrud is amongst one of the most talented &amp; impactful noses this generation has to offer, and his impressive portfolio apart from Imagination further proves that. If this man had no budget limitations with natural raw materials, imagine how many more masterpieces he could create.<br />
But back to the scent : <br />
The top notes are really citrus forward. The sharp, spicy &amp; lemony-fresh type from the bergamot &amp; citron. Along with that a really cooling, almost herbal &amp; minty sensation. As the opening fades (but never completely vanishes due to the excellent fixation skills) the scent gets even sharper, but in a clean &amp; slightly soapy way. The neroli which also comes close to the scent of orange blossom with that sharp fresh &amp; clean vibe becomes one of the main players here. Ginger possibly adds to the spicy, slightly peppery freshness.<br />
What makes this perfume really unique though is the tea. It just gives it all that special aromatic oomph that sets it apart from the typical generic blue genre. It‘s spicy, brightly-smoky, just deeply aromatic &amp; black tea-like. <br />
Ambroxan &amp; white musk (especially ambroxan) work as the fixatives in the base here with a soft woody layer. They hold &amp; push everything together so well without overshadowing the previously mentioned scent profile except in the late drydown in a completely soft &amp; inoffensive way ! Due to them the perfume will stay with you through at least half the day, making it the perfect all day scent. I comfortably get 8-10 hours with nice projection from just a couple sprays. Belletrud made it so the scent will always stay fresh &amp; tea-like, which I absolutely adore as a citrus &amp; tea fan ! He also proved that ambroxan can be totally fine if done right. Superambers like Ambrocenide are the real potent synthetic evil you should be looking at.<br />
So far no other supposedly similar perfume or dupe has succeeded in offering the same great experience. The blending with the synthetics was either way worse, meaning more dominant &amp; cheaper smelling or the natural citrus &amp; tea notes simply weren’t prominent &amp; fresh enough throughout the whole wear.<br />
My guess is that Belletrud is most likely using higher quality raw materials &amp; his blending skills with them are far superior. Just the perfect combination of natural &amp; synthetic.<br />
I am so grateful for this discovery &amp; will wear it for as long as it is available with great joy. Not only me, but also my environment (family, friends, coworkers &amp; even strangers !) always loves it &amp; complements me. Never been stopped more for any other fragrance. <br />
Nothing comes close to the positive Imagination that you evoke in me.<br />
I love you so much !</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2333728"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2333728#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2332911" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2292211">Sniffing Jin</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-28">10/28/24 23:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Synthetic done right.<br />
<br />
Citrus and soapy but done extremely well where it smells luxurious (I would hope so for the price point).  Some tea in the opening but shines in the dry down.  Main critique I hear is it is "basic", but I don't believe they were trying to make anything ground breaking here.  It is a clean, fresh smelling fragrance with monster performance that can be worn in virtually all occasions.  I have never experienced a freshie with this level of performance.<br />
<br />
Nuclear projection and lasts 10-12 hours.  People who claim it only lasts 2-4 hours need to get their noses checked.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2330966"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2330966#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2329501" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2327726"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2327726#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2327690" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2327690" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ALakota"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1565541.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ALakota" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Precious-Liquid/Salt-Pepper-80626.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.80626.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Salt & Pepper"title="Salt & Pepper"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2327690ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2327690" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541">ALakota</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-25">10/25/24 17:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I had this for some time, but I sold the 200mL bottle for a fortune because other fresh scents appealed to me more (Salt &amp; Pepper and Elysium cologne and parfum, which I'm still obsessed with and layer the three often). I recently was recommended Montagne Imaginary Pineapple, which is crazy because they are a little-known clone house primarily, but I guess they are getting more popular. I ordered a couple 50mL bottles, and I do like it a whole lot. It is supposed to be a hybrid of Imagination and Aventus Cologne, but to me it is a lot closer to Imagination because of the prominent and enduring neroli and tea notes. Off the top it smells more citrusy than at any other time, but there is a tiny hint of Aventus DNA that sticks around. Mostly in the air, I would have a tough time telling it from Imagination, but I don't have the bottle anymore to compare. Though I can't make a direct side-by-side comparison, it is quite like a more masculine take on Imagination that smells slightly less soapy and a little more citrus and maybe woody. Personally, I'm sure I prefer it, just because I can remember the extent to which I felt Imagination was so light and soapy, while IP is slightly more grounded and not as overpowered by neroli by balancing it with citrus that they call mandarin in the notes. The performance of IP seems on the caliber of Imagination, probably just because the nature of this DNA seems relatively robust. I don't want to go on forever, and I'm sure there are plenty of Imagination clones people might recommend, buy I was extremely impressed with IP, and personally prefer it because of it's balance in what I feel like is a more masculine scent, and of equal quality to LVI in terms of it's appeal and performance. I know a lot of people are purists, and ordinarily I am, and I am seriously reluctant to wear clones unless it is something unquestionably exceptional, but anyone who wants an extremely high quality scent in the realm of Imagination for about 10% of the price should at least sample Imaginary Pineapple. If you are a super enthusiast and have the cash, I do recommend Imagination, as long as you are aware that it is an extremely soapy and clean scent that smells like its price in that regard. It is about as unisex as it comes, bordering on feminine, and IP is similar in that regard. I have also heard women say that they are not a fan of such heavy neroli because it either smells too mature feminine and reminds them of older women in their lives. It is just subjective, but Imagination is something so expensive that you're going to want to sample it regardless.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2327690"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2327690#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2326481" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2250883">fbrsmells</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-24">10/24/24 15:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is perfection in a bottle. <br />
<br />
The opening starts with like a soft but still nice citrus which isnt harsh unlike many others. When it starts drying down 30 min earlier u get this really luxurious soap feel which is impossible to hate. It smells oceany soapy and a tad bit of citrus. The performance is exactly what u want not to strong but noticable. I get 16-17 hours longevity.<br />
<br />
<br />
Smell-10<br />
Performance-10<br />
Price 3/10<br />
But definitely worth it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2326481"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2326481#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2326461" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2326461" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Michael the smeller :)"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2297902"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2297902.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Michael the smeller :)" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2326461ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2326461" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2297902">Michael the smeller :)</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-24">10/24/24 14:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Imagination by Louis Vuitton is a wonderful scent with a price tag to match. I always told myself I wouldn’t spend over $200 on a fragrance, especially from a brand as luxurious (and, admittedly, snobby) as Louis Vuitton. But that changed when I visited their store to try some of their scents.<br />
<br />
At the time, I was deep into the fragrance hype around Ombre Nomade, and I’ve always loved citrus scents, so Afternoon Swim was on my radar. My fiancée and I visited the LV store near opening, and it was nearly empty, giving us plenty of time to explore. Out of the 12 scents we tried, the only one that stood out was Imagination. It's an incredible blend of citrus, fresh, floral, and other beautifully balanced notes.<br />
<br />
This fragrance has become my most-worn scent of the year, and it has truly set the bar for me. I’ve smelled over 300 fragrances from decants to niche brands, but nothing has left an impact like LV Imagination. It’s the perfect scent. At $350, it’s absolutely worth it — in fact, I’d even pay $700 for it. I understand the price tag might be a dealbreaker for some, but if you love light, inoffensive fragrances, give this one a try. And please, skip the $40 decants — this one deserves the full experience.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2326461"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2326461#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2325562" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2324868" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Fragrance_Nolan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1947453"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1947453.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Fragrance_Nolan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2324868ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2324868" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1947453">Fragrance_Nolan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-23">10/23/24 07:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I just wanted to chime in bc I see there is the thinking about Imagination smelling similar to Uden. I own a full bottle of Imagination and I used to own a full bottle of Uden. They are completely different especially the citruses. The citrus in Uden is built alongside woody and vanilla notes which comes off as a tart citrusy scent like getting wafts of a lemon meringue pie. In Imagination the citrus seems like it was constructed in a very isolated manner, and is very clean like a fresh bar of soap. The only reason there could be the slightest of resemblance between both could be that there is supposedly Guaiac wood in both formulations and pairing that with the citrus could give off a similar scent profile, but I'm personally not getting that. They are completely different and I doubt anyone getting wafts of both scents would feel any different. They are both beautiful formulations however.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2324868"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2324868#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2323677" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2323677" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Rickycorro20"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1906821"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1906821.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Rickycorro20" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Hugo-Boss/Boss-Bottled-Elixir-84074.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.84074.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Boss Bottled Elixir"title="Boss Bottled Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2323677ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2323677" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1906821">Rickycorro20</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-22">10/22/24 06:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Imagination es una de esas fragancias que me sorprendió por su elegancia discreta. Al probarla, lo que más me impactó fue su capacidad para ser fresca y ligera, pero con una profundidad inesperada. La apertura cítrica es luminosa y chispeante, pero lo que realmente me atrapó fue la transición hacia el corazón más sofisticado con té negro y neroli. Esa combinación le da un toque único que lo diferencia de otros perfumes frescos más convencionales.<br />
<br />
El fondo amaderado con ambroxan e incienso le aporta una calidez suave, lo que hace que la fragancia se sienta bien estructurada y duradera sin ser pesada. Me encanta cómo se asienta en la piel, dejando una estela que se percibe como refinada pero sin esfuerzo.<br />
<br />
Es un perfume que siento ideal para el día a día, especialmente en primavera o verano, cuando quieres algo que te refresque pero que también tenga un aire de lujo sutil. No es una fragancia intensa ni abrumadora, y eso es lo que la hace especial: su versatilidad y la sensación de llevar algo exclusivo sin ser pretencioso.<br />
<br />
En resumen, *Imagination* me parece perfecta para quien busca una fragancia sofisticada, fresca y con un toque de originalidad. Si disfrutas de los perfumes con notas cítricas y un fondo amaderado pero delicado, es una excelente opción.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2323677"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2323677#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2322494" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; STOP DOING THAT.<br />
That is not how your fragrance smells. That is not how people will smell your fragrance. Your fragrance will EVAPORATE off the surface you sprayed it on into the air around you, which is what you should try to smell.<br />
Spray it on clothing or paper and leave it in a closed room for 10-20-30-90-240-600 ( or however many, depending which stage you want to smell) minutes and then come back to it every now and then.<br />
You can thank me now.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2322494"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2322494#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2322451" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1206247">CChanel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-17">10/17/24 00:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ir really lacks wow factor if you are acquainted with perfumes from the past and even J. Cavallier style.<br />
Imagination has a lot in common with the old Versache Dreamer - the atmosphere of these perfumes is the same. Imagination is made with expensive moderns materials.<br />
I do not deny that it's a good perfume (all LV perfumes are very good), I got compliments when I wore it.<br />
<br />
J. Cavallier told in the interviews that he creates for LV, it's the style of LV not his own.<br />
<br />
Imagination - modernised Versache The Dreamer<br />
Meteore - expensive CK one<br />
Immensite - fresh YSL Rive Gauche (by the same Cavallier).<br />
<br />
You can feel that LV going towards more fresher mainstream scents, made with expensive materials. Discontinuing characteristic ones (Dans la peau, Turbulences, Contre Moi, Mille Feux) and freshening, brightening current ones (Matiere Noire is not the same as it used to be).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/887288">RMB18</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-12">10/12/24 00:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>No one talks about how close this one is to Xerjoff Uden. If you take the Rum, vanilla, coffee, and gourmand notes from uden and replace them with ambroxan and musk, you get Imagination. The same citrus note in uden is used in the opening of this. It smells incredibly clean from opening to dry down. <br />
<br />
People say this is generic, but the citrus isn't reminiscent of a generic aquatic. The citrus notes are almost identical to uden but with a different backbone. <br />
<br />
It lasts a long time especially for an aquatic. It doesn't seem to project far but the sillage is very good and people will smell you when you walk by. Whether or not you like the scent, other people will.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2312903"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2312903#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2311926" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2307604" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="IdanD"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2279089"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="IdanD" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2307604ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2307604" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2279089">IdanD</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-07">10/07/24 05:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I bought Imagination after seeing all the hype on social media. The description sounded like the kind of fragrance I’d love, and since I already own Afternoon Swimming from Louis Vuitton (which I absolutely adore), I thought this would be another safe bet.<br />
<br />
When I first visited the boutique, I had already been exposed to many scents, and my nose was overwhelmed. I did note that Ombre Nomade was too strong for me, but I didn’t fully appreciate what Imagination smelled like in that moment. Nonetheless, I decided to go ahead with the purchase.<br />
<br />
At home, I sprayed it on and, honestly, I didn’t notice anything special right away. It smelled clean, like fresh soap, but that was it. <br />
Performance-wise, it felt pretty generic, and after a couple of hours, I didn’t think it had any lasting presence.<br />
<br />
A few days later - I realized I was wrong.  Since then, I’ve worn Imagination several times, and I’ve completely fallen in love with it. It feels fresh and clean on my skin, and the number of compliments I get is absolutely ridiculous. It’s a neutral, versatile scent that’s perfect for everyday wear.<br />
<br />
In my opinion, the hype is fully justified. <br />
Indeed, the price is certainly high. But when compared to other perfumes (like those from Xerjoff, which I find strong and aggressive), Imagination is light, fresh, and very wearable. I love wearing it to work, to the gym, and even on a warm evening out with friends.<br />
<br />
In short, Imagination has won me over completely.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2307604"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2307604#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2307555" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Nice clean spring/summer scent but you could definitely find better for half the price. 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2304537"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2304537#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2304488" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2304488" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Pick"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2040463"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Pick" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2304488ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2304488" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2040463">Pick</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-04">10/04/24 06:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I want to start off by saying something that's crucial for this review, there does not exist a perfect scent.<br />
Just like food, a scent can only be so good, sauvage is good, imagination might be a bit better for certain people, but do not expect to be blown away by it. <br />
<br />
Now regarding the scent, this is intensely fresh and spicy, the citron in the top smells generically citrusy with a hint of black tea in the background.<br />
If you leave it dry down a bit it becomes a lot more spicy and soapy, it's that gingery peppery spiciness that's not uncommon in other popular colognes but still very pleasant <br />
Despite the many notes listed this is best described as a peppery ginger ambergris-like soap.<br />
<br />
Now onto the negatives.<br />
This is painfully generic, in the air, in the dry down, this could seriously be mistaken for any cheap neroli scent.<br />
It's best described as a take on the tygar and sauvage DNA, definitely different but still has many similarities, it's as if the spicy citrus ambroxan-heavy character of both was modified with a neroli and black tea backbone <br />
It smells good without a doubt but in my opinion way too generic to be worth someone's rent and have this much hype online.<br />
I see people who always bash on designer scents talk about great this is when imo it smells like sauvage and not even that much higher quality. It reminds of rich people who will try their hardest to convince themselves that balsamic glazed deconstructed gold-plated caviar tastes better than any Domino's pizza.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
There is a dupe from Zara - Sunset on the Red Sand Dune<br />
<br />
I would advise you try it cause if you're the lucky ones it will feel the same for you, which means money saved.<br />
Unfortunately everyone is different and for me and many others although the dry down is incredibly similar, I get nauseous and cannot wear it all day like with Imagination.<br />
<br />
There's a reason fragrances command such a high market price and much like wine, food and even water some people can taste the difference while others can't. Now you can say you have a more "defined palette" or "receptive sense of smell" but that is coping words for you will have to pay more to get enjoyment, cause the real reason to wear fragrances is how it smells to you, while others can be blissfully unaware.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2283358" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Wafflepuffs"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1517239"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Wafflepuffs" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2283358ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2283358" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1517239">Wafflepuffs</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-15">09/15/24 03:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Truly something special.<br />
On paper, the tea comes off way too strong with the neroli. In the opening it smells quite sharp, even after it dries down, it isn't all that special, but when you catch whiffs of it in the air, it's truly something special.<br />
I brushed it off at first thinking it was an overpriced scent that smelled nothing like what I was into,<br />
but once I caught whiffs in the air, here and there for the next few hours, It's the most soothing citrus/neroli/tea scent. Moreover, the longevity is great, and the sillage is perfect: just enough that it isn't screaming at people's faces, but not quiet enough that it goes unnoticed. And people go nose-blind to the whiffs after a few minutes so it doesn't come off as obnoxious or headache-inducing. In the air, it's soothing and appealing. <br />
A light floral aromatic backed by tea. Incredibly beautiful in the air.<br />
With the scent, longevity, and sillage, I think the insane price is quite justified and look forward to buying it in the coming months; It isn't like other LV fragrances where only a certain note of the fragrance is good, nor is the performance bad, and for that reason, I think the tag is justified.<br />
<br />
I also think it's perfectly unisex, there's the rather serious qualities from the tea, but there's also the fresh and clean floral from the neroli—perfectly unisex.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Hours will go by and I will catch whiffs quite often of it throughout the day and I seem to never go nose blind to this one.<br />
<br />
This one is more unisex. It's not masculine. <br />
<br />
As for the smell itself- it literally reminds me of floating in a cloud. Not on the cloud, but in the cloud. If you could breathe in and smell what floating on a cloud on a sunny blue skied day would smell like, Imagination would be it. It almost smells like clean laundry, but this is not exactly a fresh linen smell (well, maybe it is, sort of). It's honestly just a fresh clean smell with a strong projection. I don't know how else to put it. I don't get the citrus at all. I can see why people would also say this smells like soap, but it's better than that. Whatever it is, it's a great smell, and it lasts a long time. Get a decant if you're not sure- I know of a few sites that sell them.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2279665"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2279665#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2279100" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2276677" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jambu"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1474763"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1474763.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="jambu" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2276677ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2276677" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1474763">jambu</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-09">09/09/24 04:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I made a review for this a couple of weeks ago saying this is mid and smells like an orange peel. I changed my mind.<br />
<br />
Yes the opening does smell like an orange peel. But it's amazing. But after an hour or so you get the tea note and it smells great. <br />
<br />
I do think that this fragrance will grow on you over time, even if you were not amazed by it the first time. <br />
This is one of those scents where it makes you smell naturally good. <br />
<br />
However, there are complications for the performance with various batches. My batch (4F01) performs very well, but I have read people saying that their batch isn't performing well at all. I also do have a decant of this (4F02) and it performs just as well, but I think my bottle has a slightly sweet lying undertone that is not present with my decant. These inconsistencies is one of the problems LV has and has made me rethink my decision on whether to pull the trigger on this or not. <br />
<br />
If you are unsure whether to get a full bottle of this or not due to inconsistency issues I'd say do it now. Both my batches 4F01 and 4F02 (June and July respectively) have great performance. Unsure if there is an August batch yet, just try and request for these 2 batches in store if possible. <br />
<br />
Overall this is a great fragrance and will be my new signature for the daytime.<br />
<br />
Scent 5/5<br />
Performance 4.5/5<br />
Price 2/5<br />
3.8/5 (only because of the price, almost perfect score if you don't mind it)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2276677"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2276677#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2275890" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; But I still bought a 200ml bottle just to see if it was really worth the hype.<br />
<br />
Fast forward today and about 75ml+ down in about 2 months, I have to say this has CONSISTENTLY been my go to reach daily. The scent isn't something special. It's soapy, fresh, clean, and I do like the tea. It's a crowd pleaser. But what makes this so good is exactly that, it's so easy to reach. It's absolutely inoffensive.<br />
<br />
Have a long car ride with your mom who has a sensitive nose, but you still want to wear a fragrance? Imagination.<br />
Need something to wear to work but the entire office is full of Karens with sensitive noses? Imagination.<br />
<br />
It's such a safe, love scent for everybody. I can't imagine a single person actually disliking this scent.<br />
<br />
9/10 scent, 10/10 wearability, anytime, anywhere.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2272561"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2272561#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2271467" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2271467" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SonOfUhh"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2214516"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2214516.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SonOfUhh" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Parfums-Dusita/Issara-36485.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.36485.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Issara"title="Issara"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2271467ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2271467" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2214516">SonOfUhh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-04">09/04/24 11:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I thought I had found my signature scent, but now I cannot unsmell the "luxury soap". <br />
 <br />
The opening is citrus to ginger to tea. It's not overly sweet, its balanced and has just the right amount of floral for me. The transition into the drydown is the citrus making way for the woody notes and I get a hint of cinnamon at the back of my throat. It's all very pleasant and uniquely fresh and clean.<br />
<br />
Once completely settled, I get TEA. Tea and ginger. Tea and tiny bit of citrus. Tea making way for the wood but only for a moment. Tea and soap. Don't get me wrong, it smells good! It smells like a bar of soap at a fancy hotel; however, at the end of my second wear I was done. <br />
<br />
Performance is amazing, I was very impressed. Maybe that's why I got sick of the fragrance on me. It projects very well and lasts forever, damn near 24 hours. <br />
<br />
After first wear, I really thought I had found something special. It was fresh yet comforting and very pleasant. This is absolutely worth a try, just not for me. <br />
<br />
TL;DR - A familiar smell, mass appealing but not generic, black tea soap, crazy performance, I got sick of it quick but I hope you don't.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2262439" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Fragrance_Nolan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1947453"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1947453.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Fragrance_Nolan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2262439ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2262439" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1947453">Fragrance_Nolan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-27">08/27/24 06:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was on the fence about Imagination, but there's something about LV's fragrances that always draws me back in. Imagination smells like a very luxurious soap. If you wear this you're going to give off fresh and clean vibes. My only issue with Imagination is that it is a little too piercing and heavy, if you wear this out people are going to notice you 100% of the time, which you may not always want. I think Imagination is one of the best fresh-fragrances on the market, but given that it is a little too piercing and heavy you may want to reserve it for special occasions or when you want to make an impression.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2262439"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2262439#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2262106" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2262106" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ClosetGeek"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1458476"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="ClosetGeek" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2262106ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2262106" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1458476">ClosetGeek</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-26">08/26/24 20:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>You either like a fragrance or you don't.  From there, it's simply a matter of what you can afford and what you are willing to pay.  Regardless of either, I do not believe that price is a reason to dislike or speak against a fragrance.  <br />
<br />
This is Louis Vuitton.  A company that sells $300 keychains so you know what to expect even considering anything from this brand.  <br />
<br />
Imagination smells really good.  Period.  I have a full bottle purchased from the LV website with a July24 batch code.  Two sprays on my forearm seemed to fully project for at least two hours and I could detect it as more of a sillage for a total of about 5 hours.  I went to a movie and wore long sleeves and then not long to bed after that.  I mention those two things because the sleeve rubbing against my arm and the covers from the bed did not rub the scent off.  The next morning, exactly 15 hours later, I could smell it on my arm, albeit a skin scent.  <br />
<br />
For what one could argue is a pure summer freshie, 2 hours of projection and 5 hours of a lingering scent is frankly closer to normal than not.  However....I wore this to work today.  Two sprays behind each ear and one spray on each of my inner elbows.  I work in an office and it was nearly a 100 degree day.  This juice was fully radiating, that I could detect for 2 to 3 hours.  With certain movements, I spelled this scent all day, which I interpret as sillage.  How far, I couldn't tell, that is until I walked up to a coworker outside and from a distance of about 4 to 5 feet, she commented and complimented the fragrance.  This was 6 hours into the day and I asked if she could really smell that and she replied yes, and it's very strong in a good way and that it's very fresh smelling.  She had no idea what I was wearing. Again, this was outdoors.  And in my work vehicle with the air conditioner on, I would get whiffs of the fragrance throughout the balance of the day.  There is absolutely no doubt that I get a minimum of 8 hours of performance from Imagination before turning into a skin scent, which I believe might last another 6 or 7 hours.  I do not feel that this is a beast mode room filling fragrance by any means but I definitely believe it's noticeable by people nearby for a full work day.  I also believe that those who are complaining about performance either haven't actually tried it or have only tried a small decant with a too small atomizer.  I first tried a decant months ago and while the same scent, it's not as full as the full bottle atomizer.  <br />
<br />
Someone that does not like this simply does not like freshies.  So why even offer an opinion.  I'm not suggesting that everyone must love it and buy it.  But to say it doesn't smell good and that it's a horrible fragrance based off of price and supposed performance is just nuts.  I get why people like to use the reference of "luxury soap" but that severely understates this fragrance.  For those familiar, Prada L'homme is a classy, sunny summer Saturday morning in a white tee or untucked white button up with light blue jeans and white sneakers.  Imagination is this wearing a Rolex, driving a Mercedes coupe.  Not because it's Louis Vuitton but because of how it smells.  To be clear, it smells nothing like Prada L'homme.  It just has that same fresh vibe but is a lot smoother and without the powder.  <br />
<br />
This is not a complex scent by any stretch.  The change of notes is subtle.  Just enough to keep it from being linear.  But that is the beauty of Imagination.  Simple.  Elegant.  Luxurious.  Fresh.  Bright.  In my opinion, absolutely worth the price for a full bottle if you can afford it.  In my collection of about 60 fragrances, I have 5 fragrances that I consider elite.  This makes number 6.  But it's the only one that I would actually wear every day during the day.  <br />
<br />
Hope this helps.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2262106"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2262106#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2262008" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2259292" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="graffiti island23"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1571384"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="graffiti island23" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2259292ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2259292" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1571384">graffiti island23</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-24">08/24/24 05:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've had my bottle of Louis Vuitton Imagination for almost five months now, purchased directly from the LV store. Unfortunately, the performance has been incredibly disappointing. I get maybe 30 minutes of soft projection before it starts to fade, and within three hours, it becomes a close skin scent.<br />
<br />
If you're considering buying this fragrance, I strongly recommend avoiding retail and looking for an older batch from a few years ago. Despite letting the bottle mature and allowing air to get in, there’s been no improvement in performance. In fact, I suspect that my bottle has a higher alcohol concentration compared to a decant I have, which is likely from an older batch. That decant gives me fantastic projection and longevity, lasting over eight hours—something this newer bottle can't come close to.<br />
<br />
Lesson learned: If a fragrance is hyped up, it’s probably been reformulated to the point where it’s not worth the purchase anymore. You're better off hunting down older batches.<br />
<br />
Shame on me for falling for the hype.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2259292"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2259292#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2257344" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2257344" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="HOD6IE"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2169807"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2169807.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="HOD6IE" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.67370.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Imagination"title="Imagination"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2257344ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2257344" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2169807">HOD6IE</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-22">08/22/24 09:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>LV Imagination is a modern masterpiece in my opinion. It’s a freshy, but a unique freshy, with the combination of citrus, ginger, and black tea resulting in an incredibly pleasing and uplifting scent.<br />
<br />
On to the negatives…I’d had a few samples of this over the past few months, and finally decided to purchase a 100ml bottle direct from LV, this also came with a couple of samples, one of which being an additional 2ml of Imagination, so naturally I used up that sample prior to starting on the full bottle… I must be honest here, the performance of the sample vs the full bottle is night and day! The sample is very strong, with both great projection and longevity, whereas the performance of the full bottle juice is severely lacking!<br />
<br />
I did a batch check of the sample (4A02-Jan 2024) vs the 100ml bottle (4D01-April 2024) - I don’t want to start speculating about reformulations/batch variances etc. but did wonder if given how fresh my bottle is it may require time to macerate/develop? I’m going to do just that, it certainly can’t hurt I guess.<br />
<br />
Overall, an incredible fragrance, signature scent worthy, but disappointed in the performance of my recent April 2024 bottle – Fingers crossed that I see an improvement when I revisit it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1202859">Schmellin_Good</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-11">08/11/24 18:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Update 8/11/24: <br />
Over the last month the strength/performance has improved significantly. The batch I ended up with definitely needs to age a bit. I probably used about 10% of the bottle in the first week due to over spraying to compensate for the weak performance. I'm sure this helped since a higher air to juice ratio leads to quicker "aging".<br />
<br />
7/8/24:<br />
I've sampled Imagination a few times. Bought 2mls twice from reputable decant sellers and sampled it at an LV store. All 3 had very good performance. Lasted most of the day and even stayed on clothes after a wash cycle.<br />
<br />
The new bottle I just bought, at the LV store so it is authentic, lasts at most 90 minutes until it is barely able to be detected. Similar to the performance of an eau de cologne or body mist. Even while it is detectable, it's extremely faint. Absolutely nothing like the other "batches" I tried.<br />
<br />
Has anyone else experienced this with Imagination recently?<br />
<br />
I am thinking of taking it back to the store to exchange for another bottle. Will they even do that? If not, I may insist on being refunded.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2246235"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2246235#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2244120" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2169860">Trench1419!</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-07">08/07/24 16:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>We have this week of no sales tax, that I guess happens every year and ends tomorrow. I didn't know anything about it until just a few days ago, but that's why I went and bought a bottle of Imagination today after work. <br />
<br />
It was the first fragrance that I ever tried at the Louis Vuitton store; this was like my ninth or tenth visit. I'm not sure. I've had a sample of Imagination for a while, and I already knew I really like the scent.  It has a nice, fresh uplifting scent that seems to last all day for me, kinda like Pacific Chill without the green apple, but with black pepper or tea or something; I'm not really sure, but they seem similar to me, but obviously different enough to warrant buying them both.<br />
<br />
It doesn't have as strong of an orange top note, like Afternoon Swim, but it does have this aroma that reminds me of the pool.  I sprayed it on my arms, but I also tried a few others at the store, like Les Sables Roses and Fleur du Desert.<br />
<br />
This time, I got three free samples, including two that I didn't already have. I got a second Meteorè, and a Nouveau Monde and Orage.  I talked to the nice lady at the store about fragrances, while the bottle I bought was getting wrapped up for me. It was a nice visit. I'm planning on visiting the Louis Vuitton store up in Michigan in a few weeks, and trying the Extrait fragrances, that they don't have at the store near me.
