padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2231410" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SunnyLFL"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2205737"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="SunnyLFL" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2231410ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2231410" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2205737">SunnyLFL</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-27">07/27/24 19:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I recently tried Louis Vuitton Imagination, and my feelings about this fragrance are somewhat mixed. At first, the opening wasn't quite to my taste the strong notes of cinnamon and citrus were a bit overpowering. It felt like the cinnamon was a bit over the top, clashing with the sharpness of the citrus.<br />
<br />
However, once the initial burst settled down, the fragrance transformed into something much more enjoyable. It evolved into a light, pleasant scent that felt very wearable and comfortable. The blend became more harmonious, offering a subtle complexity that I found quite appealing.<br />
<br />
One of the standout features of Louis Vuitton Imagination is its longevity. It lasts impressively long, easily going for 9 hours on my skin, which is a huge plus. The overall scent is good, although it doesn’t break new ground in terms of uniqueness or innovation. It’s a well-crafted fragrance, but not something that feels revolutionary.<br />
<br />
Interestingly, I've received several compliments while wearing it. One person even mentioned that I smelled "clean, like soap," which I take as a positive remark. It seems to have a mass appeal, leaning towards a fresh and clean vibe that many find pleasant.<br />
<br />
In conclusion, I would recommend trying Louis Vuitton Imagination before committing to a full bottle. It's a good scent with great longevity, but its price tag might not justify the purchase for everyone. It’s definitely worth sampling to see if it aligns with your personal preferences and is a fit for your fragrance collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2231410"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2231410#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2231015" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2231015" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="LuaLat"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662645"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="LuaLat" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2231015ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2231015" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662645">LuaLat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-27">07/27/24 09:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The only fragrance I recommend from Louis Vuitton. A summer freshie that has depth and uniqueness whilst still maintaining its mass appeal. Intense blast of citron, elegant neroli, ginger and mandarin blended with wonderful strong black tea note on top of an Ambroxan musky base with warm cinnamon and a hint of Smokey woodiness to produce a wonderful, bright, uplifting, heavenly scent with warmth and depth. The Ambroxan used here is uniquely smooth and high quality so it does not have that sharp synthetic feel that it has in other fragrances but still provides a very pleasant aroma and kick. Nice airy feel to it to give this frag lift and a slight soapyness without being synthetic really adds on to the freshness. <br />
<br />
At the opening the citrus is very very zesty and pulpy almost to the point where it is unpleasant but once settled it is softer and sweeter and smells like real freshly squeezed orange. One of the most realistic citrus fragrances you will ever smell. The quality of this fragrance is also very good as it should be and the formulation consists of a high amount of naturals meaning this aroma is very pleasant and incredibly smooth with a natural aroma/feel. I was pleasantly surprised by this scent as I don’t really like Louis Vuitton fragrances as I feel they are boring and overhyped however this one I really do like and is the only fragrance from the house that I recommend purchasing. <br />
<br />
Tea note really stands out creating a smooth, green slightly earthy natural accord that is very unique and compliments the citrus very well. <br />
<br />
Wonderful clever perfumery here with a lot of thought behind it to create such a great scent with a niche feel whilst still being mass appealing. Very fresh without being boring. Versatile as can be worn casually or to formal occasions, very classy scent.<br />
<br />
Performance <br />
<br />
On my skin performs really well with <br />
10+ hours longevity on skin and around 1 or 2 days on clothes with strong projection and a nice silage trail. Performs really well on my skin especially for a freshie <br />
<br />
Whilst this is best in summer it can be worn all year round for any occasion. This isn’t outstanding but I do really like it and recommend purchasing it if you are looking for a great summer scent or all year round safe scent that is enjoyable and great quality. If you like this scent then you should definitely pick it up as it is one of the better freshies on the market. 100ml £255 200ml £375 this fragrance is more on the expensive side but isn’t the most expensive fragrance on the market and is still cheaper than a few niche brands. 9.5/10 absolutely incredible</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It's the kind of a chillingly fresh scent that makes the hair on your back/arms/legs stand on end. The quality is exceptional as well, it doesn't feel synthetic and its very well blended.<br />
I don't live in the west and don't give a shit about LV, nor have I bought anything LV, but this scent.... You can't deny the beauty of it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2228055"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2228055#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2226617" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Initially, the scent came off as harshly chemical and soapy to my nose, quite far from the described scent pyramid. I find it more acceptable now, but it still smells like rubbing a soap bar on dry skin.<br />
<br />
Overall, while it’s an acceptable scent, I find it way too overpriced for what it delivers. It’s not much of a compliment getter nor a unique scent that would be a head-turner, unless the person actually knows the scent and associates it with the brand. It feels more like a “I don’t have much time to shower” scent :). For those who enjoy this scent, I’d recommend looking into clones that are 95% similar and much more affordable.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2226210"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2226210#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2225105" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Especially since I love Pacific Chill and also like L'Immensite well enough...<br />
<br />
I did not like Imagination at all.  I don't know what it was, but I almost got something in the opening that was peppery which turned me off.  Also if I didn't know it was LV(like a blind sniff test), I would have thought this was some synthetic cheapo.<br />
<br />
Everyone talks about how LV Imagination has a "je ne sais quoi" that makes it amazing or "too unique to describe, you just have tk smell it".  Well I did and whatever that something is that ppl seem to love, just isn't for me.<br />
<br />
I think all LV fragrance is overrated and overpriced but I'd still pay for another bottle of Pacific Chill.  So glad I didn't waste the money on more than just a few ml.  I think that if one is going to spend this type of bread there are much much better choices around.<br />
<br />
Save your money</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2223298"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2223298#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222947" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2221788" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JasKiew"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1611442"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1611442.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JasKiew" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Lattafa-Perfumes/Al-Nashama-Caprice-89764.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.89764.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Al Nashama Caprice"title="Al Nashama Caprice"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2221788ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2221788" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1611442">JasKiew</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-17">07/17/24 19:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sunrise On The Red Sand Dunes Zara vs Imagination Louis Vuitton<br />
<br />
Sunrise Zara opens more citrusy and pronounces loudly to the wearer in the initial 5 to 10 minutes with a blast of zesty citrusy orange, so aromatic and fresh. After that it calms down and becomes really close to Imagination.<br />
<br />
Whereas Imagination doesn't open loudly, it remains pretty much the same from the opening to the mids but on the immediate opening spray you'll be able to get the Neroli in it too. Not for the case of Sunrise Zara.<br />
<br />
Sunrise Zara doesn't have the nice neroli in imagination and it's orangey cirtusy dna remains to mid. Basically for the Sunrise you'll get a distinguished mandarin orange, orange blossom and black current. Whereas on imagination, you'll get the nice Chinese black tea c02 and Tunisian neroli, Sicilian cedar and ambrox. That's probably the main differences. I'll say give and take 60-70% somewhat similarities.<br />
<br />
Imagination seems more polarizing as the scent develops into a more musculine with cedar dna while the sunrise Zara remains orangey flora and stays linear to me.<br />
<br />
Overall I think it's a good alternative despite not so close for $49.90 Singapore dollars. It's good enough to be a scent on its own and smells really nice, doesn't need the comparison to Imagination. Suits our Sunny warm humid weather out here. Generally lasts up to half a day out there or perhaps longer in Air-conditioning. Imagination does smells more classy and better quality and goes in a different direction with the tea and neroli.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2221788"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2221788#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2221653" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
LV has really done something special with Imagination. It is a very alluring and captivating smell; unique but familiar at the same time. Citrus, neroli, and tea, with some mild spices. this, L’Immensité and Pacific Chill are my favourites. <br />
<br />
Is it overpriced? Yes... but oh does it smell amazing. With all honesty I don't think there is a better "soapy" scent out on the market. The amber is very prominent in this one. I'm not sure why it's marketed for men because this equally could be pulled off by women.<br />
<br />
I truly believe that if this was more affordable it would be way way way more popular even though it is kinda hyped right now. <br />
<br />
This doesn't radiate off my skin at all, just leaves an amazing scent trail when I walk by so if you're looking for something that's more out there probably skip this one. You will be noticed when you walk by but it's not strong enough to "fill the room". <br />
<br />
Longevity; about 4 hours of scent trail then dies down to a skin scent that lasts about 12 hours which is good enough for me. Looking at the other freshies in the market it's honestly hard to find something longer lasting than that unless you're looking at Sauvage which is godly in terms of performance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Longevity is amazing, and although projection dies down after the first few hours, I can smell this on skin the next day which is unreal for a fragrance this fresh. <br />
<br />
I find it so calming, and when I wear it, I can't stop smelling it. It's been a long time since a fragrance captivated me in this way.<br />
<br />
I had to get a bottle, I love it. <br />
<br />
Ps, the clones don't cut it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2217749"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2217749#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2217089" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1903875">hokeypokeyguy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-12">07/12/24 22:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have a sample of this, along with Météore and Afternoon Swim. I like this one! <br />
<br />
So, the sillage is good, which should be expected from LV. Unfortunately, the longevity is subpar, which is a pattern we see from LV sometimes. Don't give up on this one in the opening...wait a few minutes for the dry down and you'll realize why so many people like it!<br />
<br />
I personally think this one leans more male, but not far from unisex. If a girl wore this, I feel like it would be pretty normal. On my skin, it's a bit hard for me to pick up but it's still detectable. Maybe I'm just noseblind, who nose.<br />
<br />
Price: $320 USD.<br />
<br />
Scary...would I pay that? <br />
<br />
Yes. though the longevity is poor you can always reapply, and spray accordingly. Something people tend to always forget with fragrances is you need to use your sprays according to the strength of the fragrance. This fragrance has good sillage luckily, but if you want that sillage to last longer, you can absolutely do more sprays than usual.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Step into the boutique you're greeted and attended to like a celeb or royalty (I'm not).  It's all done so well. There's bound to be a loading in the price for this fuss.<br />
<br />
Imagination is an ethereal, airy, dreamy citrus, with enduring performance, albeit limited sillage.  I still got wafts for hours.  It is very lovely.<br />
<br />
But for the asking price I'd expect knee buckling, eye rolling, have to sit down to take it in, gorgeousness.  Whilst being so lovely, and very wearable it does NOT meet this demanding standard.  Therefore a like rather than a love.<br />
<br />
I confess to finding the tea note overly subtle.  Tea lovers with a citrus note might want to try Jul Et Mad's Aqua Sextius which IMO is a superior fragrance.<br />
<br />
3.5/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2215562"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2215562#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2215499" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1725959">XGR04</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-03">07/03/24 11:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I must preface this review by saying that I've never really been one for citrusy, summery fragrances, and tend to get bored of most very quickly!<br />
<br />
The opening of this fragrance, on my skin, is rather pleasant, if unremarkable. The citron, bergamot and orange notes quickly subside, paving their way to the heart notes of Imagination. In the heart, I mainly detect the notes of neroli - which creates a distinct "soapiness" - and cinnamon, with a slight touch of ginger. The cinnamon note reminds me of that used in MFK's Oud Satin Mood Extrait; dusty, sweet, and slightly spicy in nature. Regarding the base, I can only really detect the tea accord and guaiac wood note.<br />
<br />
So, do I enjoy it?<br />
<br />
Somewhat, although I find it to be linear and lack depth. One of the things I've noticed each time I've worn it is that, without fail, I continue to draw associations between it and the clean, synthetic smell of bathrooms (especially those in upmarket shopping centres, hotels, and even those in international airports). These are all scents that I actually quite enjoy, though would not want to smell on myself for obvious reasons. It's a real shame, as this tends to stay on my skin for upwards of twelve hours, with good projection for the first four.<br />
<br />
What I really dislike about Imagination, however, is the price that Louis Vuitton commands for it. I would be lying if I claimed that Imagination is worth even half of its current RRP. Nothing about this fragrance warrants a price tag even remotely close to what it is now... for goodness sake, there are artisanal houses that produce similarly-priced perfumes that are far superior! My point still stands in relation to the rest of the Estée Lauder and LVMH-owned fragrance houses, although that's really a story for another day.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2207135"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2207135#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2206654" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Stillage-7 <br />
Longevity-8</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2205983"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2205983#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2205325" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2205325" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ClosetGeek"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1458476"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="ClosetGeek" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2205325ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2205325" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1458476">ClosetGeek</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-01">07/01/24 21:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Follow up to my post about a month ago....<br />
<br />
Eight sprays, three behind each ear and one on each forearm at 6am.  Very noticeable to me for two or three hours and I would assume projecting beyond an arms reach at least.  I would get periodic, less prominent whiffs for the balance of the day, but I would assume still getting slight projection within an arms reach along with decent sillage.  At 6pm, I was laying on the couch and when I would turn my head from one side to the other, I would get faint whiffs of Imagination.  Despite still being able to detect the fragrance, I'm assuming that after 12 hours, it's little more than a strong skin scent, which was still present on my forearm when holding it up to my nose.  <br />
<br />
However.....I went to my son's baseball game at 7pm, and sat next to my ex who immediately commented that I smell good.  Shocked, I asked if she could still smell that and she replied "Yes, very much so.  It smells really good."  Granted, a total of 6 sprays on my neck and out in open air with a slight breeze helped the fragrance along, but to be that detectable after more than 12 hours, breeze or not is quite amazing.  And her comment really made me wonder how much it was projecting in the morning.  <br />
<br />
If you are familiar with BR540, which I also own, then you know that while very fleeting to the wearer, it's has high projection and strong sillage.  I do not think LV Imagination performs as prominently but I do believe it wears cleaner and lighter and performs similarly.  We all get different mileage and the best advice I can give is to sample it for yourself.  But while not always obvious to me that it's present, much like BR540, I have no question that on my skin, LV Imagination is not only on my skin for at least 12 hours, but projects well for at least a full, in office work day.  <br />
<br />
Comments have been made about this fragrance being linear.  I won't make such a claim but I do understand why some say that.  But IMO, there is a place in the world for a simple, clean, light fragrance such as LV Imagination.  It's far from complex, far from dense, far from niche as you can get.  But to use terms like shower gel and soap are very misleading.  This is an elite fragrance among the likes of YSL Tuxedo, BR540 among others.  I've read a few comments comparing this to Guerlain Ideal Platine Prive', which I also own, and Imagination is nothing close in terms of fragrance and especially quality.  <br />
<br />
If I'm going to argue being overpriced, then that's going to be a general argument for any fragrance quite frankly.  I really wonder if people would feel as strongly if this were available in a 50 or 75ml bottle and priced accordingly.  Regardless, after today's wearing, I have decided to buy a full bottle.  It fills a specific "need" in my collection and I not  only love the fragrance but I also love how it makes me feel wearing it in the morning.<br />
<br />
One final update since this post yesterday:  I wore LV Imagination again today with the same 8 sprays, hugged a friend 3 hours later with a general compliment, "You smell good".  An hour later, she sent a text to say I smell "too good" and she could still smell it.  I'm not sure what "too good" is but I do know what sillage is, and apparently, this juice has plenty of it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2205325"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2205325#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2204860" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2202137" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="wjh"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1918328"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="wjh" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2202137ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2202137" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1918328">wjh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-28">06/28/24 10:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I think this serves as the perfect example of feeling let down by an overly hyped fragrance. Don't get me wrong; it's a pleasant perfume. It's a refreshing option for spring and summer. However, after seeing it highly praised across numerous platforms, I may have set my expectations too high.<br />
<br />
To me, the scent is rather linear. I primarily pick up notes of citrus and ginger throughout its duration.<br />
<br />
As for its longevity, I'm not impressed. I'm left to wonder if it fades on my skin too quickly, never really reaching the full dry-down. For the price point, I certainly expect better performance.<br />
<br />
If you like Imagination but find yourself disappointed in it's performance and simplicity, I would recommend checking out Vibrato by Sospiro. Not the same scent but similar vibes and the projection and longevity on Vibrato is outstanding. I also find it to be a more interesting DNA. <br />
<br />
To summarize, although it presents a very fresh and mass appealing option for warmer weather, I find that, due to its lackluster staying power and simplicity, it doesn't justify the cost.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2202137"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2202137#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2201659" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Quality of the raw materials ? Image ? Ego trip ? Not sure if it's my skin chemistry, but this seems to last FOREVER on me. With moderate projection also. <br />
It got to a point where it was giving me a headache. I don't think I can wear this daily.<br />
But the quality of the frag is there and it's worth it if you can buy it. They've managed to retain many volatile citrus notes, far more than any of my other frags, which makes it keep its bright charm for long. There's masterclass perfumery at play.<br />
Plus you get the LV clout (which is probably why you bought it in the first place).<br />
Is it overpriced? Yes. Is it amazing? Yes.<br />
9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="2201483"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=2201483#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2200904" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; LV makes awesome scents that aren’t too polarizing and are extremely high quality. As I’ve said before, these aren’t made for collectors. They’re made for the average LV customer who is used to spending lots of money on luxury goods. So I think this is priced just right and if the note breakdown intrigues you; then give it a try! I NEVER wear fragrances for compliments and I really don’t believe anything I read but my wife and women seem to love this one. Imagination takes the modern blue series trend up by 2 new levels. Ambroxan base throughout the life but kicks off with the freshest of sweet tea and bitter citron. Settles into a nuanced sweet neroli and cinnamon twist. Imagine a creamy breakfast pastry garnished with a citrus glaze on on a warm summer morning in Ischia. A unique experience but one that’ll leave you thoroughly impressed. This is the definition of modern fragrance refined.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="1473429"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=1473429#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1923717" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1923717" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="WhiteFlowerPrincess"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662712"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1662712.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="WhiteFlowerPrincess" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Lucky-48385.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48385.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Lucky"title="Lucky"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1923717ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1923717" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662712">WhiteFlowerPrincess</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-09">09/09/23 11:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got a sample of this fragrance with a bunch of other samples of fragrances when I was shopping for clothes at Louis Vuitton.<br />
<br />
It's unusual that they gave me a men's fragrance to sample, but I really like this as a fragrance for men! (Not for me though, of course. It would be too masculine for me to wear personally. I'd say it is a masculine leaning unisex fragrance.) <br />
<br />
It is very fresh and citric smelling right off the bat from the citron, bergamot and orange notes. It's very invigorating too. I can also smell the zingy and spicy ginger in this and the bitter and lightly floral neroli also. It makes me think of the Mediterranean Sea and orange and other citrus groves, so I get a very blue feeling from Imagination.<br />
<br />
Further into the middle of this perfume and into the dry down I can smell the sweet, green and herbaceous smell of tea and it gives me a very zen-like, aromatic and calming quality to me. All of this combined with the citruses conjures up an image of a devastatingly handsome and fabulously wealthy man with wavy brown hair drinking a cup of tea while on his yacht on Lake Como, gazing out at the citrus trees while wearing a pair of black sunglasses, a blue buttoned-down collared shirt, a pair of white shorts and a pair of white moccassins.<br />
<br />
The ambroxan in the drydown was a bit too much for me though and it made me think of cheaper aquatic/blue men's fragrances in the 1990s like Davidoff Cool Water. This is my only criticism of this otherwise fantastic fragrance though. The sweetness from the tea and olibanum notes softened the edges from the ambroxan somewhat thankfully.<br />
<br />
Sillage was moderate and its longevity was surprisingly long lasting, lasting about 8 hours in total. It's a slightly overpriced fragrance, but it is still worth it for a man to buy for himself or for a woman like me to buy for a special man in her life... 8.5/10 from me!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="1923717"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=1923717#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="67370" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

No definitely not.<br />
<br />
The scent is very very hyped as I see, so when I got it opened the box and sprayed immediately on my skin.. which I could not smell so I sprayed like 4 times more and it started to project a bit. First impression: Sweet Lipton ice tea sparkle. The lemon was so synthetic and had a strange background to it.. it’s like bitter yet warm sweet.. like rose lemon kind of a thing… anyways, later on it’s the neroli who steals the show het then again before it becomes a real white detergent scent that ice tea note pops up and kills it for me. If you want tea notes in perfume.. check on mefisto, silver mountain water or even woolong cha. This is a perfume which was definitely not finished from a Artis view.. such a shame, the lemon could be sharper, less warm, less ambroxan and more neroli with maybe some juniper? <br />
<br />
Anyways it smells different enough and not as some would say a typical blue, because it’s absolutely not a blue scent.. but if you are in to detergent scents.. check on MFK gentle fluidity silver, roja Oceania, viking cologne.. or if you are crazy about tea notes? Check on smw or mefisto gentluomo these are the top notch. <br />
<br />
Again this is a unfinished mess without having a clear vision. I understand the audience of Louis Vuitton, but you can’t just ask 240€ for this quality, I mean it’s unfinished smells like “no vision”.. I’m really impressed as well how people can hype this, maybe I should borrow their noses for a day. <br />
<br />
3/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="67370"comment_id="1727250"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Imagination-67370.html?ccid=1727250#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1677945" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
